## License Compliance

All data is used in accordance with the respective licenses of each repository. Most awesome lists are licensed under Creative Commons or MIT licenses, which permit this type of usage with.

## Contributing

If you are a maintainer of one of these repositories and have any concerns about how your data is being used, please open an issue in our repository.

## Thank You

Special thanks to the awesome list community and particularly to [sindresorhus/awesome](https://github.com/sindresorhus/awesome) for starting the awesome list movement.
